The 2006 Formula One season was the 59th season of Formula One motor racing. The season began on 18 March at the Australian Grand Prix and ended on 27 November at the Brazilian Grand Prix.
The 2006 season was the first season since 1994 to feature a new set of regulations, the "FIA Formula One Sporting Regulations 2006". The regulations were designed to reduce the aerodynamic downforce of the cars, and to increase the importance of mechanical grip. The regulations also introduced a new tyre supplier, Bridgestone, replacing Michelin.

The Argentine Polo Association (Asociación Argentina de Polo) is the governing body for the sport of polo in Argentina. It was founded in 1950 and is based in Buenos Aires.

Scotturb Bus 403 is a bus route operated by Scotturb in Lisbon, Portugal. It runs from the city centre to Cabo da Roca, the westernmost point of continental Europe.
The route is operated by a fleet of 12 Mercedes-Benz O405D buses.
